    24	  initValue,
    25	  setBindingSerializedValue,
    26	} from "../util/signals";
    27	import translateVar from "../util/translate-var";
    28	
    29	declare module "@marko/compiler/dist/types" {
    30	  export interface NodeExtra {
    31	    static?: boolean;
    32	  }
    33	}
    34	
    35	export default {
    36	  analyze(tag: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag>) {
    37	    const { node } = tag;
    38	    const tagVar = node.var;
    39	    let valueAttr: t.MarkoAttribute | undefined;
    40	    let valueChangeAttr: t.MarkoAttribute | undefined;
    41	    for (const attr of node.attributes) {
    42	      if (t.isMarkoAttribute(attr)) {
    43	        if (attr.name === "value") {
    44	          valueAttr = attr;
    45	        } else if (attr.name === "valueChange") {
    46	          valueChangeAttr = attr;
    47	        } else {
    48	          const start = attr.loc?.start;
    49	          const end = attr.loc?.end;
    50	          const msg =
    51	            "The `let` tag only supports the `value` attribute and its change handler.";
    52	
    53	          if (start == null || end == null) {
    54	            throw tag.get("name").buildCodeFrameError(msg);
    55	          } else {
    56	            throw tag.hub.buildError(
    57	              { loc: { start, end } } as unknown as t.Node,
    58	              msg,
    59	              Error,
    60	            );
    61	          }
    62	        }
    63	      }
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    assertNoArgs(tag);
    67	    assertNoParams(tag);
    68	    assertNoBodyContent(tag);
    69	    assertNoSpreadAttrs(tag);
    70	
    71	    if (!tagVar) {
    72	      throw tag
    73	        .get("name")
    74	        .buildCodeFrameError("The `let` tag requires a tag variable.");
    75	    }
    76	
    77	    if (!t.isIdentifier(tagVar)) {
    78	      throw tag
    79	        .get("var")
    80	        .buildCodeFrameError("The `let` tag variable cannot be destructured.");
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    if (valueChangeAttr && computeNode(valueChangeAttr.value)) {
    84	      throw tag
    85	        .get("attributes")
    86	        .find((attr) => attr.node === valueChangeAttr)!
    87	        .get("value")
    88	        .buildCodeFrameError(
    89	          "The `let` tag `valueChange` attribute must be a function.",
    90	        );
    91	    }
    92	
    93	    const tagSection = getOrCreateSection(tag);
    94	    const binding = trackVarReferences(tag, BindingType.let)!;
    95	    setBindingValueExpr(
    96	      binding,
    97	      mergeReferences(tagSection, tag.node, [
    98	        valueAttr?.value,
    99	        valueChangeAttr?.value,
   100	      ]),
   101	    );
   102	
   103	    if (valueChangeAttr) {
   104	      // TODO: could be based on if there are actually assignments.
   105	      forceBindingSerialize(
   106	        tagSection,
   107	        binding,
   108	        getAccessorPrefix().TagVariableChange,
   109	      );
   110	    }
   111	  },
   112	  translate: {
   113	    exit(tag) {
   114	      const { node } = tag;
   115	      const tagVar = node.var!;
   116	      const valueAttr =
   117	        node.attributes.find(
   118	          (attr) =>
   119	            t.isMarkoAttribute(attr) && (attr.default || attr.name === "value"),
   120	        ) ?? t.markoAttribute("value", t.identifier("undefined"));
   121	      const valueChangeAttr = node.attributes.find(
   122	        (attr) => t.isMarkoAttribute(attr) && attr.name === "valueChange",
   123	      );
   124	      const section = getSection(tag);
   125	      const binding = tagVar.extra!.binding!;
   126	
   127	      if (isOutputDOM()) {
   128	        const signal = initValue(binding, "state");
   129	        const referencedBindings = tag.node.extra!.referencedBindings;
   130	
   131	        addValue(section, referencedBindings, signal, valueAttr.value);
   132	
   133	        if (valueChangeAttr) {
   134	          signal.extraArgs = [valueChangeAttr.value];
   135	        }
   136	
   137	        signal.buildAssignment = (valueSection, value) => {
   138	          const scope = getScopeExpression(valueSection, signal.section);
   139	
   140	          return t.callExpression(signal.identifier, [scope, value]);
   141	        };
   142	      } else {
   143	        translateVar(tag, valueAttr.value, "let");
   144	
   145	        if (valueChangeAttr) {
   146	          setBindingSerializedValue(
   147	            section,
   148	            binding,
   149	            valueChangeAttr.value,
   150	            getAccessorPrefix().TagVariableChange,
   151	          );
   152	        }
   153	      }
   154	
   155	      tag.remove();
   156	    },
   157	  },
   158	  parseOptions: {
   159	    openTagOnly: true,
   160	  },
   161	  attributes: {},
   162	  autocomplete: [
   163	    {
   164	      description: "Use to create a mutable binding.",
   165	      descriptionMoreURL: "https://markojs.com/docs/core-tags/#let",
   166	    },
   167	  ],
   168	  types: runtimeInfo.name + "/tags/let.d.marko",
   169	} as Tag;
   170

    50	        );
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    const valueExtra = evaluate(valueAttr.value);
    54	    const upstreamAlias = t.isIdentifier(valueAttr.value)
    55	      ? tag.scope.getBinding(valueAttr.value.name)?.identifier.extra?.binding
    56	      : undefined;
    57	
    58	    if (upstreamAlias) {
    59	      valueExtra.pruned = true;
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    const binding = trackVarReferences(tag, BindingType.derived, upstreamAlias);
    63	
    64	    if (binding) {
    65	      if (!valueExtra.nullable) binding.nullable = false;
    66	      setBindingValueExpr(binding, valueExtra);
    67	      valueExtra.downstream = {
    68	        bindings: binding,
    69	        excludeProperties: undefined,
    70	      };
    71	    }
    72	  },

    82	
    83	        if (varBinding && !varBinding.upstreamAlias) {

     1	import { types as t } from "@marko/compiler";
     2	
     3	import { forEachIdentifierPath } from "./for-each-identifier";
     4	
     5	export default function translateVar(
     6	  tag: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag>,
     7	  initialValue: t.Expression,
     8	  kind: "let" | "const" = "const",
     9	) {
    10	  const {
    11	    node: { var: tagVar },
    12	  } = tag;
    13	
    14	  if (!tagVar) {
    15	    return;
    16	  }
    17	
    18	  forEachIdentifierPath(tag.get("var"), (id) => {
    19	    const binding = id.node.extra?.binding;
    20	    if (
    21	      !binding ||
    22	      !binding.upstreamAlias ||
    23	      !binding.assignmentSections ||
    24	      id.node === tagVar
    25	    ) {
    26	      return;
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    const changeName = binding.name + "Change";
    30	    const changeBinding = binding.upstreamAlias.propertyAliases.get(changeName);
    31	    if (changeBinding && changeName !== changeBinding.name) {
    32	      // add a new property to the destructure list when a change handler is implicitly added
    33	      // eg by assigning to a destructured property.
    34	      getDestructurePattern(id)?.pushContainer(
    35	        "properties",
    36	        t.objectProperty(
    37	          t.identifier(changeName),
    38	          t.identifier(changeBinding.name),
    39	        ),
    40	      );
    41	    }
    42	  });
    43	
    44	  tag.insertBefore(
    45	    t.variableDeclaration(kind, [t.variableDeclarator(tagVar, initialValue)]),
    46	  );
    47	}
    48	
    49	function getDestructurePattern(id: t.NodePath<t.Identifier>) {
    50	  let cur: t.NodePath | null = id;
    51	
    52	  while (cur) {
    53	    if (cur.node.type === "ObjectPattern") {
    54	      return cur as t.NodePath<t.ObjectPattern>;
    55	    }
    56	    cur = cur.parentPath;
    57	  }
    58	}
    59

import translator from "@marko/runtime-tags/translator";

const code = `
export interface Input {
  duration: number;
  value: () => void;
}

<let/timer=(0 as unknown as ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>)>

    clearTimeout(timer);

  timer = setTimeout(() => {
    input.value();
  }, input.duration);
}>

<return=reset>

     2	  let i = 0;
     3	  for (const attr of path.node.attributes) {
     4	    if (attr.type === "MarkoSpreadAttribute") {
     5	      throw path.hub.buildError(
     6	        attr,
     7	        `Tag does not support spread attributes.`,
     8	      );
     9	    } else if (!allowed.includes(attr.name)) {
    10	      throw path.hub.buildError(
    11	        attr,
    12	        `Tag does not support the \`${attr.name}\` attribute.`,
    13	      );
    14	    }
    15	
    16	    i++;
    17	  }
    18	}

    11	import { isOutputDOM } from "../util/marko-config";

    25	  setBindingSerializedValue,
    26	} from "../util/signals";
    27	import translateVar from "../util/translate-var";
    28	
    29	declare module "@marko/compiler/dist/types" {
    30	  export interface NodeExtra {
    31	    static?: boolean;
    32	  }
    33	}
    34	
    35	export default {
    36	  analyze(tag: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag>) {
    37	    const { node } = tag;
    38	    const tagVar = node.var;
    39	    let valueAttr: t.MarkoAttribute | undefined;
    40	    let valueChangeAttr: t.MarkoAttribute | undefined;
    41	    for (const attr of node.attributes) {
    42	      if (t.isMarkoAttribute(attr)) {
    43	        if (attr.name === "value") {
    44	          valueAttr = attr;
    45	        } else if (attr.name === "valueChange") {
    46	          valueChangeAttr = attr;
    47	        } else {
    48	          const start = attr.loc?.start;
    49	          const end = attr.loc?.end;
    50	          const msg =
    51	            "The `let` tag only supports the `value` attribute and its change handler.";
    52	
    53	          if (start == null || end == null) {
    54	            throw tag.get("name").buildCodeFrameError(msg);
    55	          } else {
    56	            throw tag.hub.buildError(
    57	              { loc: { start, end } } as unknown as t.Node,
    58	              msg,
    59	              Error,
    60	            );
    61	          }
    62	        }
    63	      }
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    assertNoArgs(tag);
    67	    assertNoParams(tag);
    68	    assertNoBodyContent(tag);
    69	    assertNoSpreadAttrs(tag);
    70	
    71	    if (!tagVar) {
    72	      throw tag
    73	        .get("name")
    74	        .buildCodeFrameError("The `let` tag requires a tag variable.");
    75	    }
    76	
    77	    if (!t.isIdentifier(tagVar)) {
    78	      throw tag
    79	        .get("var")
    80	        .buildCodeFrameError("The `let` tag variable cannot be destructured.");
    81	    }
    82	
    83	    if (valueChangeAttr && computeNode(valueChangeAttr.value)) {
    84	      throw tag
    85	        .get("attributes")
    86	        .find((attr) => attr.node === valueChangeAttr)!
    87	        .get("value")
    88	        .buildCodeFrameError(
    89	          "The `let` tag `valueChange` attribute must be a function.",
    90	        );
    91	    }
    92	
    93	    const tagSection = getOrCreateSection(tag);
    94	    const binding = trackVarReferences(tag, BindingType.let)!;
    95	    setBindingValueExpr(
    96	      binding,
    97	      mergeReferences(tagSection, tag.node, [
    98	        valueAttr?.value,
    99	        valueChangeAttr?.value,
   100	      ]),
   101	    );
   102	
   103	    if (valueChangeAttr) {
   104	      // TODO: could be based on if there are actually assignments.
   105	      forceBindingSerialize(
   106	        tagSection,
   107	        binding,
   108	        getAccessorPrefix().TagVariableChange,
   109	      );
   110	    }
   111	  },
   112	  translate: {
   113	    exit(tag) {
   114	      const { node } = tag;
   115	      const tagVar = node.var!;
   116	      const valueAttr =
   117	        node.attributes.find(
   118	          (attr) =>
   119	            t.isMarkoAttribute(attr) && (attr.default || attr.name === "value"),
   120	        ) ?? t.markoAttribute("value", t.identifier("undefined"));
   121	      const valueChangeAttr = node.attributes.find(
   122	        (attr) => t.isMarkoAttribute(attr) && attr.name === "valueChange",
   123	      );
   124	      const section = getSection(tag);
   125	      const binding = tagVar.extra!.binding!;
   126	
   127	      if (isOutputDOM()) {
   128	        const signal = initValue(binding, "state");
   129	        const referencedBindings = tag.node.extra!.referencedBindings;
   130	
   131	        addValue(section, referencedBindings, signal, valueAttr.value);
   132	
   133	        if (valueChangeAttr) {
   134	          signal.extraArgs = [valueChangeAttr.value];
   135	        }
   136	
   137	        signal.buildAssignment = (valueSection, value) => {
   138	          const scope = getScopeExpression(valueSection, signal.section);
   139	
   140	          return t.callExpression(signal.identifier, [scope, value]);
   141	        };
   142	      } else {
   143	        translateVar(tag, valueAttr.value, "let");
   144	
   145	        if (valueChangeAttr) {

   147	            section,
   148	            binding,
   149	            valueChangeAttr.value,
   150	            getAccessorPrefix().TagVariableChange,
   151	          );
   152	        }
   153	      }
   154	
   155	      tag.remove();
   156	    },
   157	  },

   159	    openTagOnly: true,

   147	const [getBindings] = createProgramState(() => new Set<Binding>());
   148	const [getNextBindingId, setNextBindingId] = createProgramState(() => 0);
   149	export function createBinding(
   150	  name: string,
   151	  type: Binding["type"],
   152	  section: Section,
   153	  upstreamAlias?: Binding["upstreamAlias"],
   154	  property?: string,
   155	  excludeProperties?: Opt<string>,
   156	  loc: t.SourceLocation | null = null,
   157	  declared = false,
   158	): Binding {
   159	  const id = getNextBindingId();
   160	  const binding: Binding = {
   161	    id,
   162	    name,
   163	    type,
   164	    loc,
   165	    section,
   166	    property,
   167	    declared,
   168	    closureSections: undefined,
   169	    assignmentSections: undefined,
   170	    excludeProperties,
   171	    sources: undefined,
   172	    aliases: new Set(),
   173	    hoists: new Map(),
   174	    propertyAliases: new Map(),
   175	    upstreamAlias,
   176	    downstreamExpressions: new Set(),
   177	    scopeOffset: undefined,
   178	    export: undefined,
   179	    nullable: excludeProperties === undefined,
   180	  };
   181	
   182	  if (property) {
   183	    if (declared) upstreamAlias!.nullable = false;
   184	    // TODO: should prefer declared properties as alias roots.
   185	    const propBinding = upstreamAlias!.propertyAliases.get(property);
   186	    if (propBinding) {
   187	      binding.property = undefined;
   188	      binding.upstreamAlias = propBinding;
   189	      propBinding.aliases.add(binding);
   190	    } else {
   191	      // TODO: check if default is used, if so an intermediate binding is needed
   192	      upstreamAlias!.propertyAliases.set(property, binding);
   193	    }
   194	  } else if (upstreamAlias) {
   195	    upstreamAlias.aliases.add(binding);
   196	  }
   197	
   198	  setNextBindingId(id + 1);
   199	  getBindings().add(binding);
   200	  return binding;
   201	}

   203	export function trackVarReferences(
   204	  tag: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag>,
   205	  type: BindingType,
   206	  upstreamAlias?: Binding["upstreamAlias"],
   207	) {
   208	  const tagVar = tag.node.var;
   209	  if (tagVar) {
   210	    let canonicalUpstreamAlias = getCanonicalBinding(upstreamAlias);
   211	    if (canonicalUpstreamAlias) {
   212	      const { excludeProperties } = canonicalUpstreamAlias;
   213	      if (excludeProperties !== undefined) {
   214	        canonicalUpstreamAlias = canonicalUpstreamAlias.upstreamAlias!;
   215	      }
   216	      createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   217	        tagVar,
   218	        canonicalUpstreamAlias.type,
   219	        tag.scope,
   220	        canonicalUpstreamAlias.section,
   221	        canonicalUpstreamAlias,
   222	        undefined,
   223	        excludeProperties,
   224	      );
   225	      return canonicalUpstreamAlias;
   226	    }
   227	
   228	    createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   229	      tagVar,
   230	      type,
   231	      tag.scope,
   232	      getOrCreateSection(tag),
   233	      undefined,
   234	      undefined,
   235	      undefined,
   236	    );
   237	    return tagVar.extra?.binding;
   238	  }
   239	}

   241	export function trackParamsReferences(
   242	  body: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTagBody | t.Program>,
   243	  type: BindingType,
   244	  upstreamAlias?: Binding["upstreamAlias"],
   245	) {
   246	  const params = body.node.params;
   247	  if (body.node.body.length && params.length) {
   248	    const canonicalUpstreamAlias = getCanonicalBinding(upstreamAlias);
   249	    let section: Section;
   250	    if (canonicalUpstreamAlias) {
   251	      section = canonicalUpstreamAlias.section;
   252	      type = canonicalUpstreamAlias.type;
   253	    } else {
   254	      section = getOrCreateSection(body);
   255	    }
   256	    const paramsBinding =
   257	      canonicalUpstreamAlias ||
   258	      ((body.node.extra ??= {}).binding = createBinding(
   259	        generateUid("params"),
   260	        type,
   261	        section,
   262	        undefined,
   263	        undefined,
   264	      ));
   265	
   266	    section.params = paramsBinding;
   267	
   268	    for (let i = 0; i < params.length; i++) {
   269	      const param = params[i];
   270	      if (param.type === "RestElement") {
   271	        createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   272	          param.argument,
   273	          type,
   274	          body.scope,
   275	          section,
   276	          paramsBinding,
   277	          undefined,
   278	          addNumericPropertiesUntil(undefined, i - 1),
   279	        );
   280	      } else if (t.isLVal(param)) {
   281	        createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   282	          param,
   283	          type,
   284	          body.scope,
   285	          section,
   286	          paramsBinding,
   287	          i + "",
   288	          undefined,
   289	        );
   290	      }
   291	    }
   292	
   293	    return paramsBinding;
   294	  }
   295	}

   297	export function trackHoistedReference(
   298	  referencePath: t.NodePath<t.Identifier>,
   299	  binding: Binding,
   300	) {
   301	  const section = binding.section;
   302	  const referenceSection = getOrCreateSection(referencePath);
   303	  const hoistSection = getCommonSection(referenceSection, section);
   304	  const extra = (referencePath.node.extra ??= {});
   305	
   306	  let hoistedBinding = binding.hoists.get(hoistSection);
   307	  if (!hoistedBinding) {
   308	    binding.hoists.set(
   309	      hoistSection,
   310	      (hoistedBinding = createBinding(
   311	        generateUid("hoisted_" + referencePath.node.name),
   312	        BindingType.hoist,
   313	        hoistSection,
   314	        undefined,
   315	        undefined,
   316	        undefined,
   317	        binding.loc,
   318	        true,
   319	      )),
   320	    );
   321	
   322	    section.hoisted = bindingUtil.add(section.hoisted, binding);
   323	
   324	    let currentSection = section.parent;
   325	    while (currentSection && currentSection !== hoistSection) {
   326	      currentSection.isHoistThrough = true;
   327	      currentSection = currentSection.parent;
   328	    }
   329	  }
   330	
   331	  if (isInvokedFunction(referencePath)) {
   332	    extra.read = createRead(hoistedBinding, undefined);
   333	    extra.section = referenceSection;
   334	    extra[kIsInvoked] = true;
   335	  } else {
   336	    trackReference(referencePath, hoistedBinding);
   337	  }
   338	
   339	  referenceSection.referencedHoists = bindingUtil.add(
   340	    referenceSection.referencedHoists,
   341	    hoistedBinding,
   342	  );
   343	}
   344	
   345	function trackReferencesForBinding(babelBinding: t.Binding, binding: Binding) {
   346	  const { referencePaths, constantViolations } = babelBinding;
   347	
   348	  for (const referencePath of referencePaths) {
   349	    const referenceSection = getOrCreateSection(referencePath);
   350	    if (isSameOrChildSection(binding.section, referenceSection)) {
   351	      if (
   352	        binding.type === BindingType.local &&
   353	        referenceSection === binding.section
   354	      ) {
   355	        continue;
   356	      }
   357	      trackReference(referencePath as t.NodePath<t.Identifier>, binding);
   358	    } else {
   359	      trackHoistedReference(referencePath as t.NodePath<t.Identifier>, binding);
   360	    }
   361	  }
   362	
   363	  for (const ref of constantViolations) {
   364	    if (ref.isUpdateExpression()) {
   365	      trackAssignment(ref.get("argument"), binding);
   366	    } else if (ref.isAssignmentExpression()) {
   367	      trackAssignment(ref.get("left"), binding);
   368	
   369	      if (ref.node.operator !== "=") {
   370	        /*
   371	         * https://github.com/babel/babel/issues/11313
   372	         * We need this so we can handle `+=` and friends
   373	         */
   374	        const left = ref.get("left");
   375	        if (left.isIdentifier()) {
   376	          trackReference(left, binding);
   377	        }
   378	      }
   379	    }
   380	  }
   381	}
   382	
   383	function trackAssignment(
   384	  assignment: t.NodePath<
   385	    t.AssignmentExpression["left"] | t.UpdateExpression["argument"]
   386	  >,
   387	  binding: Binding,
   388	) {
   389	  const fnRoot = getFnRoot(assignment);
   390	  const fnExtra = fnRoot && ((fnRoot.node.extra ??= {}) as FnExtra);
   391	  const section = getOrCreateSection(assignment);
   392	  setReferencesScope(assignment);
   393	  forEachIdentifierPath(assignment, (id) => {
   394	    if (id.node.name === binding.name) {
   395	      const extra = (id.node.extra ??= {}) as AssignedBindingExtra;
   396	
   397	      if (binding.upstreamAlias && binding.property !== undefined) {
   398	        const changePropName = binding.property + "Change";
   399	        const changeBinding =
   400	          binding.upstreamAlias.propertyAliases.get(changePropName) ||
   401	          createBinding(
   402	            generateUid(changePropName),
   403	            BindingType.derived,
   404	            binding.section,
   405	            binding.upstreamAlias,
   406	            changePropName,
   407	            undefined,
   408	            id.node.loc,
   409	            true,
   410	          );
   411	        extra.assignmentTo = changeBinding;
   412	        addReadToExpression(id, changeBinding);
   413	      }
   414	
   415	      binding.assignmentSections = sectionUtil.add(
   416	        binding.assignmentSections,
   417	        section,
   418	      );
   419	      extra.assignment = binding;
   420	      extra.section = section;
   421	      extra.fnExtra = fnExtra;
   422	    }
   423	  });
   424	}
   425	
   426	export function setReferencesScope(path: t.NodePath<any>) {
   427	  const fnRoot = getFnRoot(path);
   428	  if (fnRoot) {
   429	    (fnRoot.node.extra ??= {}).referencesScope = true;
   430	  }
   431	}
   432	
   433	function createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   434	  lVal: t.LVal,
   435	  type: BindingType,
   436	  scope: t.Scope,
   437	  section: Section,
   438	  upstreamAlias: Binding["upstreamAlias"] | undefined,
   439	  property: string | undefined,
   440	  excludeProperties: Opt<string>,
   441	) {
   442	  switch (lVal.type) {
   443	    case "Identifier":
   444	      trackReferencesForBinding(
   445	        scope.getBinding(lVal.name)!,
   446	        ((lVal.extra ??= {}).binding = createBinding(
   447	          lVal.name,
   448	          type,
   449	          section,
   450	          upstreamAlias,
   451	          property,
   452	          excludeProperties,
   453	          lVal.loc,
   454	          true,
   455	        )),
   456	      );
   457	      break;
   458	    case "ObjectPattern": {
   459	      const patternBinding =
   460	        (property
   461	          ? upstreamAlias!.propertyAliases.get(property)
   462	          : upstreamAlias) ||
   463	        ((lVal.extra ??= {}).binding = createBinding(
   464	          generateUid(property || "pattern"),
   465	          type,
   466	          section,
   467	          upstreamAlias,
   468	          property,
   469	          excludeProperties,
   470	          lVal.loc,
   471	        ));
   472	
   473	      const hasRest =
   474	        lVal.properties[lVal.properties.length - 1]?.type === "RestElement";
   475	      for (const prop of lVal.properties) {
   476	        if (prop.type === "RestElement") {
   477	          createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   478	            prop.argument,
   479	            type,
   480	            scope,
   481	            section,
   482	            patternBinding,
   483	            property,
   484	            excludeProperties,
   485	          );
   486	        } else {
   487	          let key: string;
   488	
   489	          if (prop.key.type === "Identifier") {
   490	            key = prop.key.name;
   491	          } else if (prop.key.type === "StringLiteral") {
   492	            key = prop.key.value;
   493	          } else {
   494	            // TODO: it should be a computed value
   495	            throw new Error("computed keys not supported in object pattern");
   496	          }
   497	
   498	          if (hasRest) {
   499	            excludeProperties = propsUtil.add(excludeProperties, key);
   500	          }
   501	
   502	          if (t.isLVal(prop.value)) {
   503	            createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   504	              prop.value,
   505	              type,
   506	              scope,
   507	              section,
   508	              patternBinding,
   509	              key,
   510	              undefined,
   511	            );
   512	          }
   513	        }
   514	      }
   515	      break;
   516	    }
   517	    case "ArrayPattern": {
   518	      const patternBinding =
   519	        (property
   520	          ? upstreamAlias!.propertyAliases.get(property)
   521	          : upstreamAlias) ||
   522	        ((lVal.extra ??= {}).binding = createBinding(
   523	          generateUid(property || "pattern"),
   524	          type,
   525	          section,
   526	          upstreamAlias,
   527	          property,
   528	          excludeProperties,
   529	          lVal.loc,
   530	        ));
   531	
   532	      let i = -1;
   533	      for (const element of lVal.elements) {
   534	        i++;
   535	        if (element) {
   536	          if (element.type === "RestElement") {
   537	            excludeProperties = addNumericPropertiesUntil(
   538	              excludeProperties,
   539	              i - 1,
   540	            );
   541	            createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   542	              element.argument,
   543	              type,
   544	              scope,
   545	              section,
   546	              patternBinding,
   547	              property,
   548	              excludeProperties,
   549	            );
   550	          } else if (t.isLVal(element)) {
   551	            createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   552	              element,
   553	              type,
   554	              scope,
   555	              section,
   556	              patternBinding,
   557	              `${i}`,
   558	              undefined,
   559	            );
   560	          }
   561	        }
   562	      }
   563	      break;
   564	    }
   565	    case "AssignmentPattern":
   566	      // TODO: this makes a default value an alias,
   567	      // but it really should be a computed value
   568	      createBindingsAndTrackReferences(
   569	        lVal.left,
   570	        type,
   571	        scope,
   572	        section,
   573	        upstreamAlias,
   574	        property,
   575	        undefined,
   576	      );
   577	
   578	      if (lVal.left.extra?.binding) {
   579	        (lVal.right.extra ??= {}).downstream = {
   580	          bindings: lVal.left.extra.binding,
   581	          excludeProperties: undefined,
   582	        };
   583	      }
   584	      break;
   585	  }
   586	}
   587	
   588	function trackReference(
   589	  referencePath: t.NodePath<t.Identifier>,
   590	  binding: Binding,
   591	) {
   592	  let root: t.NodePath<t.Identifier> | t.NodePath<t.MemberExpressio<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you.      1	import { types as t } from "@marko/compiler";
     2	
     3	import { forEachIdentifierPath } from "./for-each-identifier";
     4	
     5	export default function translateVar(
     6	  tag: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag>,
     7	  initialValue: t.Expression,
     8	  kind: "let" | "const" = "const",
     9	) {
    10	  const {
    11	    node: { var: tagVar },
    12	  } = tag;
    13	
    14	  if (!tagVar) {
    15	    return;
    16	  }
    17	
    18	  forEachIdentifierPath(tag.get("var"), (id) => {
    19	    const binding = id.node.extra?.binding;
    20	    if (
    21	      !binding ||
    22	      !binding.upstreamAlias ||
    23	      !binding.assignmentSections ||
    24	      id.node === tagVar
    25	    ) {
    26	      return;
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    const changeName = binding.name + "Change";
    30	    const changeBinding = binding.upstreamAlias.propertyAliases.get(changeName);
    31	    if (changeBinding && changeName !== changeBinding.name) {
    32	      // add a new property to the destructure list when a change handler is implicitly added
    33	      // eg by assigning to a destructured property.
    34	      getDestructurePattern(id)?.pushContainer(
    35	        "properties",
    36	        t.objectProperty(
    37	          t.identifier(changeName),
    38	          t.identifier(changeBinding.name),
    39	        ),
    40	      );
    41	    }
    42	  });
    43	
    44	  tag.insertBefore(
    45	    t.variableDeclaration(kind, [t.variableDeclarator(tagVar, initialValue)]),
    46	  );
    47	}
    48	
    49	function getDestructurePattern(id: t.NodePath<t.Identifier>) {
    50	  let cur: t.NodePath | null = id;
    51	
    52	  while (cur) {
    53	    if (cur.node.type === "ObjectPattern") {
    54	      return cur as t.NodePath<t.ObjectPattern>;
    55	    }
    56	    cur = cur.parentPath;
    57	  }
    58	}

     1	import { types as t } from "@marko/compiler";
     2	
     3	import { forEachIdentifierPath } from "./for-each-identifier";
     4	
     5	export default function translateVar(
     6	  tag: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag>,
     7	  initialValue: t.Expression,
     8	  kind: "let" | "const" = "const",
     9	) {
    10	  const {
    11	    node: { var: tagVar },
    12	  } = tag;
    13	
    14	  if (!tagVar) {
    15	    return;
    16	  }
    17	
    18	  forEachIdentifierPath(tag.get("var"), (id) => {
    19	    const binding = id.node.extra?.binding;
    20	    if (
    21	      !binding ||
    22	      !binding.upstreamAlias ||
    23	      !binding.assignmentSections ||
    24	      id.node === tagVar
    25	    ) {
    26	      return;
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    const changeName = binding.name + "Change";
    30	    const changeBinding = binding.upstreamAlias.propertyAliases.get(changeName);
    31	    if (changeBinding && changeName !== changeBinding.name) {
    32	      // add a new property to the destructure list when a change handler is implicitly added
    33	      // eg by assigning to a destructured property.
    34	      getDestructurePattern(id)?.pushContainer(
    35	        "properties",
    36	        t.objectProperty(
    37	          t.identifier(changeName),
    38	          t.identifier(changeBinding.name),
    39	        ),
    40	      );
    41	    }
    42	  });
    43	
    44	  tag.insertBefore(
    45	    t.variableDeclaration(kind === "let" ? "let" : "const", [
    46	      t.variableDeclarator(tagVar, initialValue),
    47	    ]),
    48	  );
    49	}
    50	
    51	function getDestructurePattern(id: t.NodePath<t.Identifier>) {
    52	  let cur: t.NodePath | null = id;
    53	
    54	  while (cur) {
    55	    if (cur.node.type === "ObjectPattern") {
    56	      return cur as t.NodePath<t.ObjectPattern>;
    57	    }
    58	    cur = cur.parentPath;
    59	  }
    60	}
    61

     1	import { types as t } from "@marko/compiler";
     2	
     3	import { forEachIdentifierPath } from "./for-each-identifier";
     4	
     5	export default function translateVar(
     6	  tag: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag>,
     7	  initialValue: t.Expression,
     8	  kind: "let" | "const" = "const",
     9	) {
    10	  const {
    11	    node: { var: tagVar },
    12	  } = tag;
    13	
    14	  if (!tagVar) {
    15	    return;
    16	  }
    17	
    18	  forEachIdentifierPath(tag.get("var"), (id) => {
    19	    const binding = id.node.extra?.binding;
    20	    if (
    21	      !binding ||
    22	      !binding.upstreamAlias ||
    23	      !binding.assignmentSections ||
    24	      id.node === tagVar
    25	    ) {
    26	      return;
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    const changeName = binding.name + "Change";
    30	    const changeBinding = binding.upstreamAlias.propertyAliases.get(changeName);
    31	    if (changeBinding && changeName !== changeBinding.name) {
    32	      // add a new property to the destructure list when a change handler is implicitly added
    33	      // eg by assigning to a destructured property.
    34	      getDestructurePattern(id)?.pushContainer(
    35	        "properties",
    36	        t.objectProperty(
    37	          t.identifier(changeName),
    38	          t.identifier(changeBinding.name),
    39	        ),
    40	      );
    41	    }
    42	  });
    43	
    44	  if (tag.node.var) {
    45	    forEachIdentifierPath(tag.get("var"), (id) => {
    46	      // Set constant to false if it's a let binding
    47	      if (kind === "let") {
    48	        tag.scope.getBinding(id.node.name).constant = false;
    49	      }
    50	    });
    51	  }
    52	
    53	  tag.insertBefore(
    54	    t.variableDeclaration(kind === "let" ? "let" : "const", [
    55	      t.variableDeclarator(tagVar, initialValue),
    56	    ]),
    57	  );
    58	}
    59	
    60	function getDestructurePattern(id: t.NodePath<t.Identifier>) {
    61	  let cur: t.NodePath | null = id;
    62	
    63	  while (cur) {
    64	    if (cur.node.type === "ObjectPattern") {
    65	      return cur as t.NodePath<t.ObjectPattern>;
    66	    }
    67	    cur = cur.parentPath;
    68	  }
    69	}

   149	function getMarkoFile(code, fileOpts, markoOpts) {
   150	  const { translator } = markoOpts;
   151	  let compileCache = markoOpts.cache.get(translator);
   152	
   153	  if (!compileCache) {
   154	    markoOpts.cache.set(translator, (compileCache = new Map()));
   155	  }
   156	
   157	  const { filename } = fileOpts;
   158	  const isSource = markoOpts.output === "source";
   159	  const isMigrate = markoOpts.output === "migrate";
   160	  const canCache = !(isSource || isMigrate);
   161	  const id = getTemplateId(markoOpts, filename);
   162	  const contentHash = canCache && new Hash().update(code).digest();
   163	  let cached = canCache && compileCache.get(id);
   164	
   165	  if (cached) {
   166	    if (cached.contentHash !== contentHash) {
   167	      // File content changed, invalidate the cache.
   168	      cached = undefined;
   169	    } else {
   170	      for (const watchFile of cached.file.metadata.marko.watchFiles) {
   171	        let mtime = Infinity;
   172	        try {
   173	          mtime = markoOpts.fileSystem.statSync(watchFile).mtime;
   174	        } catch {
   175	          // ignore
   176	        }
   177	
   178	        if (mtime > cached.time) {
   179	          // Some dependency changed, invalidate the cache.
   180	          cached = undefined;
   181	          break;
   182	        }
   183	      }
   184	    }
   185	  }
   186	
   187	  if (cached) {
   188	    return cached.file;
   189	  }
   190	
   191	  const prevFs = taglibConfig.fs;
   192	  const prevFile = getFileInternal();
   193	  taglibConfig.fs = markoOpts.fileSystem;
   194	
   195	  try {
   196	    const file = setFileInternal(
   197	      new MarkoFile(fileOpts, {
   198	        code,
   199	        ast: {
   200	          type: "File",
   201	          program: {
   202	            type: "Program",
   203	            sourceType: "module",
   204	            body: [],
   205	            directives: [],
   206	            params: [t.identifier("input")],
   207	          },
   208	        },
   209	      }),
   210	    );
   211	    file.markoOpts = markoOpts;
   212	    file.___compileStage = "parse";
   213	    file.___getMarkoFile = getMarkoFile;
   214	    const taglibLookup = (file.___taglibLookup = buildLookup(
   215	      path.dirname(filename),
   216	      translator,
   217	    ));
   218	    const meta = (file.metadata.marko = {
   219	      id,
   220	      deps: [],

   224	    });

   239	    }

   243	    traverseAll(file, rootMigrators);
   244	
   245	    if (file.___hasParseErrors) {
   246	      if (markoOpts.errorRecovery) {
   247	        t.traverseFast(file.path.node, (node) => {
   248	          if (node.type === "MarkoParseError") {
   249	            diagnosticError(file.path, {
   250	              label: node.label,
   251	              loc: node.errorLoc || node.loc,
   252	            });
   253	          }
   254	        });
   255	      } else {
   256	        let errors = [];
   257	        t.traverseFast(file.path.node, (node) => {
   258	          if (node.type === "MarkoParseError") {
   259	            errors.push(
   260	              buildCodeFrameError(
   261	                file.opts.filename,
   262	                file.code,
   263	                node.errorLoc || node.loc,
   264	                node.label,
   265	              ),
   266	            );
   267	          }
   268	        });
   269	
   270	        throwAggregateError(errors);
   271	      }
   272	    }
   273	
   274	    if (isMigrate) {
   275	      return file;
   276	    }
   277	
   278	    const rootTransformers = [];
   279	    for (const id in taglibLookup.taglibsById) {
   280	      for (const transformer of taglibLookup.taglibsById[id].transformers) {
   281	        addPlugin(meta, rootTransformers, transformer);
   282	      }
   283	    }
   284	
   285	    rootTransformers.push(transform);
   286	    if (translator.transform) {
   287	      rootTransformers.push(translator.transform);
   288	    }
   289	    file.___compileStage = "transform";
   290	    traverseAll(file, rootTransformers);
   291	
   292	    for (const taglibId in taglibLookup.taglibsById) {
   293	      const { filePath } = taglibLookup.taglibsById[taglibId];
   294	
   295	      if (
   296	        filePath[filePath.length - 5] === "." &&
   297	        filePath.endsWith("marko.json")
   298	      ) {
   299	        meta.watchFiles.push(filePath);
   300	      }
   301	    }
   302	
   303	    compileCache.set(id, {
   304	      time: Date.now(),
   305	      file,
   306	      contentHash,
   307	    });
   308	
   309	    if (translator.analyze) {
   310	      try {
   311	        file.___compileStage = "analyze";
   312	        traverseAll(file, translator.analyze);
   313	      } catch (e) {
   314	        compileCache.delete(id);
   315	        throw e;
   316	      }
   317	    }
   318	
   319	    return file;
   320	  } finally {
   321	    taglibConfig.fs = prevFs;
   322	    setFileInternal(prevFile);
   323	  }
   324	}
   325	
   326	function shallowClone(data) {
   327	  const clone = {};
   328	
   329	  for (const key in data) {
   330	    const v = data[key];
   331	
   332	    if (v !== undefined) {
   333	      if (v === null || typeof v !== "object") {
   334	        clone[key] = v;
   335	      } else {
   336	        const Ctor = v.constructor;
   337	
   338	        switch (Ctor) {
   339	          case Array:
   340	            clone[key] = [...v];
   341	            break;
   342	          case Object:
   343	          case null:
   344	            clone[key] = { ...v };
   345	            break;
   346	          case Map:
   347	          case Set:
   348	          case Date:
   349	          case RegExp:
   350	            clone[key] = new Ctor(v);
   351	            break;
   352	
   353	          default:
   354	            throw new Error(`Unsupported metadata type of ${Ctor.name}`);
   355	        }
   356	      }
   357	    }
   358	  }
   359	
   360	  return clone;
   361	}
   362	
   363	function mergeVisitors(all) {
   364	  if (Array.isArray(all)) {
   365	    if (all.length === 1) {
   366	      all = all[0];
   367	    } else {
   368	      return traverse.visitors.merge(all);
   369	    }
   370	  }
   371	
   372	  return traverse.visitors.explode(all);
   373	}
   374	
   375	function traverseAll(file, visitors) {
   376	  const program = file.path;
   377	  traverse(
   378	    program.node,
   379	    mergeVisitors(visitors),
   380	    program.scope,
   381	    (program.state = {}),
   382	    program,
   383	    true,
   384	  );
   385	}
   386	
   387	function addPlugin(meta, arr, plugin) {
   388	  if (plugin) {
   389	    const hook = plugin.hook.default || plugin.hook;
   390	
   391	    if (plugin.path) {
   392	      meta.watchFiles.push(plugin.path);
   393	    }
   394	
   395	    if (Array.isArray(hook)) {
   396	      arr.push(...hook);
   397	    } else {
   398	      arr.push(hook);
   399	    }
   400	  }
   401	}
   402	
   403	function isMarkoOutput(output) {
   404	  return output === "source" || output === "migrate";
   405	}
   406	
   407	function finalizeMeta(meta) {
   408	  meta.watchFiles = [...new Set(meta.watchFiles)];
   409	  if (meta.analyzedTags) {
   410	    meta.analyzedTags = [...meta.analyzedTags];
   411	  }
   412	}
   413

     2	export function forEachIdentifier(
     3	  node: t.Node,
     4	  cb: (identifier: t.Identifier) => void,
     5	) {
     6	  switch (node.type) {
     7	    case "ObjectPattern":
     8	      for (const prop of node.properties) {
     9	        switch (prop.type) {
    10	          case "ObjectProperty":
    11	            if (prop.value.type === "AssignmentPattern") {
    12	              forEachIdentifier(prop.value.left, cb);
    13	            } else {
    14	              forEachIdentifier(prop.value, cb);
    15	            }
    16	            break;
    17	          case "RestElement":
    18	            forEachIdentifier(prop.argument, cb);
    19	            break;
    20	        }
    21	      }
    22	      break;
    23	    case "ArrayPattern":
    24	      for (const el of node.elements) {
    25	        if (el != null) {
    26	          switch (el.type) {
    27	            case "RestElement":
    28	              forEachIdentifier(el.argument, cb);
    29	              break;
    30	            case "AssignmentPattern":
    31	              forEachIdentifier(el.left, cb);
    32	              break;
    33	            default:
    34	              forEachIdentifier(el, cb);
    35	              break;
    36	          }
    37	        }
    38	      }
    39	      break;
    40	    case "Identifier":
    41	      cb(node);
    42	      break;
    43	  }
    44	}
    45	
    46	export function forEachIdentifierPath(
    47	  nodePath: t.NodePath<any>,
    48	  cb: (identifier: t.NodePath<t.Identifier>) => void,
    49	) {
    50	  if (nodePath.isIdentifier()) {
    51	    cb(nodePath);
    52	  } else if (nodePath.isObjectPattern()) {
    53	    for (const prop of nodePath.get("properties")) {
    54	      if (prop.isObjectProperty()) {
    55	        const value = prop.get("value");
    56	        if (value.isAssignmentPattern()) {
    57	          forEachIdentifierPath(value.get("left"), cb);
    58	        } else {
    59	          forEachIdentifierPath(value, cb);
    60	        }
    61	      } else if (prop.isRestElement()) {
    62	        forEachIdentifierPath(prop.get("argument"), cb);
    63	      }
    64	    }
    65	  } else if (nodePath.isArrayPattern()) {
    66	    for (const el of nodePath.get("elements")) {
    67	      if (el) {

    69	          forEachIdentifierPath(el.get("argument"), cb);
    70	        } else if (el.isAssignmentPattern()) {
    71	          forEachIdentifierPath(el.get("left"), cb);
    72	        } else {
    73	          forEachIdentifierPath(el, cb);
    74	        }
    75	      }
    76	    }
    77	  }

     1	import { types as t } from "@marko/compiler";
     2	
     3	import { forEachIdentifierPath } from "./for-each-identifier";
     4	
     5	export default function translateVar(
     6	  tag: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag>,
     7	  initialValue: t.Expression,
     8	  kind: "let" | "const" = "const",
     9	) {
    10	  const {
    11	    node: { var: tagVar },
    12	  } = tag;
    13	
    14	  if (!tagVar) {
    15	    return;
    16	  }
    17	
    18	  forEachIdentifierPath(tag.get("var"), (id) => {
    19	    const binding = id.node.extra?.binding;
    20	    if (
    21	      !binding ||
    22	      !binding.upstreamAlias ||
    23	      !binding.assignmentSections ||
    24	      id.node === tagVar
    25	    ) {
    26	      return;
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    const changeName = binding.name + "Change";
    30	    const changeBinding = binding.upstreamAlias.propertyAliases.get(changeName);
    31	    if (changeBinding && changeName !== changeBinding.name) {
    32	      // add a new property to the destructure list when a change handler is implicitly added
    33	      // eg by assigning to a destructured property.
    34	      getDestructurePattern(id)?.pushContainer(
    35	        "properties",
    36	        t.objectProperty(
    37	          t.identifier(changeName),
    38	          t.identifier(changeBinding.name),
    39	        ),
    40	      );
    41	    }
    42	  });
    43	
    44	  tag.insertBefore(
    45	    t.variableDeclaration(kind, [t.variableDeclarator(tagVar, initialValue)]),
    46	  );
    47	}
    48	
    49	function getDestructurePattern(id: t.NodePath<t.Identifier>) {
    50	  let cur: t.NodePath | null = id;
    51	
    52	  while (cur) {
    53	    if (cur.node.type === "ObjectPattern") {
    54	      return cur as t.NodePath<t.ObjectPattern>;
    55	    }
    56	    cur = cur.parentPath;
    57	  }
    58	}
    59

     1	import { types as t } from "@marko/compiler";
     2	
     3	import { forEachIdentifierPath } from "./for-each-identifier";
     4	
     5	export default function translateVar(
     6	  tag: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag>,
     7	  initialValue: t.Expression,
     8	  kind: "let" | "const" = "const",
     9	) {
    10	  const {
    11	    node: { var: tagVar },
    12	  } = tag;
    13	
    14	  if (!tagVar) {
    15	    return;
    16	  }
    17	
    18	  forEachIdentifierPath(tag.get("var"), (id) => {
    19	    const binding = id.node.extra?.binding;
    20	    if (
    21	      !binding ||
    22	      !binding.upstreamAlias ||
    23	      !binding.assignmentSections ||
    24	      id.node === tagVar
    25	    ) {
    26	      return;
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    const changeName = binding.name + "Change";
    30	    const changeBinding = binding.upstreamAlias.propertyAliases.get(changeName);
    31	    if (changeBinding && changeName !== changeBinding.name) {
    32	      // add a new property to the destructure list when a change handler is implicitly added
    33	      // eg by assigning to a destructured property.
    34	      getDestructurePattern(id)?.pushContainer(
    35	        "properties",
    36	        t.objectProperty(
    37	          t.identifier(changeName),
    38	          t.identifier(changeBinding.name),
    39	        ),
    40	      );
    41	    }
    42	  });
    43	
    44	  if (tag.node.var) {
    45	    forEachIdentifierPath(tag.get("var"), (id) => {
    46	      // Set constant to false if it's a let binding
    47	      if (kind === "let") {
    48	        tag.scope.crawl();
    49	        const binding = tag.scope.getBinding(id.node.name);
    50	        if (binding) {
    51	          binding.constant = false;
    52	        }
    53	      }
    54	    });
    55	    tag.scope.crawl();
    56	  }
    57	
    58	  tag.insertBefore(
    59	    t.variableDeclaration(kind, [t.variableDeclarator(tagVar, initialValue)]),
    60	  );
    61	}
    62	
    63	function getDestructurePattern(id: t.NodePath<t.Identifier>) {
    64	  let cur: t.NodePath | null = id;
    65	
    66	  while (cur) {
    67	    if (cur.node.type === "ObjectPattern") {
    68	      return cur as t.NodePath<t.ObjectPattern>;
    69	    }
    70	    cur = cur.parentPath;
    71	  }
    72	}

     1	import { types as t } from "@marko/compiler";
     2	
     3	import { forEachIdentifierPath } from "./for-each-identifier";
     4	
     5	export default function translateVar(
     6	  tag: t.NodePath<t.MarkoTag>,
     7	  initialValue: t.Expression,
     8	  kind: "let" | "const" = "const",
     9	) {
    10	  const {
    11	    node: { var: tagVar },
    12	  } = tag;
    13	
    14	  if (!tagVar) {
    15	    return;
    16	  }
    17	
    18	  forEachIdentifierPath(tag.get("var"), (id) => {
    19	    const binding = id.node.extra?.binding;
    20	    if (
    21	      !binding ||
    22	      !binding.upstreamAlias ||
    23	      !binding.assignmentSections ||
    24	      id.node === tagVar
    25	    ) {
    26	      return;
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    const changeName = binding.name + "Change";
    30	    const changeBinding = binding.upstreamAlias.propertyAliases.get(changeName);
    31	    if (changeBinding && changeName !== changeBinding.name) {
    32	      // add a new property to the destructure list when a change handler is implicitly added
    33	      // eg by assigning to a destructured property.
    34	      getDestructurePattern(id)?.pushContainer(
    35	        "properties",
    36	        t.objectProperty(
    37	          t.identifier(changeName),
    38	          t.identifier(changeBinding.name),
    39	        ),
    40	      );
    41	    }
    42	  });
    43	
    44	  tag.insertBefore(
    45	    t.variableDeclaration(kind, [t.variableDeclarator(tagVar, initialValue)]),
    46	  );
    47	}
    48	
    49	function getDestructurePattern(id: t.NodePath<t.Identifier>) {
    50	  let cur: t.NodePath | null = id;
    51	
    52	  while (cur) {
    53	    if (cur.node.type === "ObjectPattern") {
    54	      return cur as t.NodePath<t.ObjectPattern>;
    55	    }
    56	    cur = cur.parentPath;
    57	  }
    58	}
